<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Timeline of European exploration</h1> <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div> <div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Emanuel_Gottlieb_Leutze_-_Columbus_Before_the_Queen.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1147" data-file-width="1536" decoding="async" height="224" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Emanuel_Gottlieb_Leutze_-_Columbus_Before_the_Queen.JPG/300px-Emanuel_Gottlieb_Leutze_-_Columbus_Before_the_Queen.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Emanuel_Gottlieb_Leutze_-_Columbus_Before_the_Queen.JPG/450px-Emanuel_Gottlieb_Leutze_-_Columbus_Before_the_Queen.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Emanuel_Gottlieb_Leutze_-_Columbus_Before_the_Queen.JPG/600px-Emanuel_Gottlieb_Leutze_-_Columbus_Before_the_Queen.JPG 2x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Emanuel_Gottlieb_Leutze_-_Columbus_Before_the_Queen.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i>Columbus before the Queen</i>, imagined by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Emanuel_Gottlieb_Leutze" title="Emanuel Gottlieb Leutze">Emanuel Gottlieb Leutze</a>, 1843</div></div></div>
<p>The following timeline covers European exploration from 1418 to 1957.
</p><p>The 15th century witnessed the rounding of the feared <a href="/wiki/Cape_Bojador" title="Cape Bojador">Cape Bojador</a> and Portuguese exploration of the west coast of Africa, while in the last decade of the century the Spanish sent expeditions to the New World, focusing on exploring the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">Caribbean Sea</a>, and the Portuguese discovered the sea route to India. In the 16th century, various countries sent exploring parties into the interior of the Americas, as well as to their respective west and east coasts north to California and Labrador and south to Chile and Tierra del Fuego. In the 17th century, the Russians explored and conquered Siberia in search of sables, while the Dutch roughly worked on the chart for Australia. The 18th century saw the first extensive exploration of the South Pacific and the discovery of Alaska, while the nineteenth was dominated by exploration of the polar regions (not to mention excursions into the heart of Africa). By the 20th century, the poles themselves had been reached.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="15th_century">15th century</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_European_exploration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: 15th century">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Vascodagama.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1302" data-file-width="670" decoding="async" height="428" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Vascodagama.JPG/220px-Vascodagama.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Vascodagama.JPG/330px-Vascodagama.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Vascodagama.JPG/440px-Vascodagama.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Vascodagama.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Vasco da Gama lands at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Calicut" title="Calicut">Calicut</a>, illustration for Os Lusíadas, 1880 by Ernesto Casanova.</div></div></div>
<ul><li>1418 – <a href="/wiki/Jo%C3%A3o_Gon%C3%A7alves_Zarco" title="João Gonçalves Zarco">João Gonçalves Zarco</a> and <a href="/wiki/Trist%C3%A3o_Vaz_Teixeira" title="Tristão Vaz Teixeira">Tristão Vaz Teixeira</a> discover <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Porto_Santo" title="Porto Santo">Porto Santo</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diffie_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-Diffie-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li>1419 – <a href="/wiki/Jo%C3%A3o_Gon%C3%A7alves_Zarco" title="João Gonçalves Zarco">Gonçalves</a> and Vaz discover <a href="/wiki/Madeira" title="Madeira">Madeira</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diffie_1-1"><a href="#cite_note-Diffie-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li>1427 – <a href="/wiki/Diogo_de_Silves" title="Diogo de Silves">Diogo de Silves</a> discovers the <a href="/wiki/Azores" title="Azores">Azores</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diffie_1-2"><a href="#cite_note-Diffie-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li>1434 – <a href="/wiki/Gil_Eanes" title="Gil Eanes">Gil Eanes</a> passes <a href="/wiki/Cape_Chaunar" title="Cape Chaunar">Cabo de Não</a> and rounds <a href="/wiki/Cape_Bojador" title="Cape Bojador">Cape Bojador</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1444 – <a href="/wiki/Dinis_Dias" title="Dinis Dias">Dinis Dias</a> reaches the mouth of the <a href="/wiki/Senegal_River" title="Senegal River">Senegal River</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitfield_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-Whitfield-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li>1446 – The <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portuguese</a> reach <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde" title="Cape Verde">Cape Verde</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Gambia_River" title="Gambia River">Gambia River</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitfield_3-1"><a href="#cite_note-Whitfield-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li>1456 – <a href="/wiki/Alvise_Cadamosto" title="Alvise Cadamosto">Alvise Cadamosto</a> and <a href="/wiki/Diogo_Gomes" title="Diogo Gomes">Diogo Gomes</a> explored the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cape_Verde_Islands" title="Cape Verde Islands">Cape Verde Islands</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diffie_1-3"><a href="#cite_note-Diffie-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li>1460 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/P%C3%AAro_de_Sintra" title="Pêro de Sintra">Pêro de Sintra</a> reaches <a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone" title="Sierra Leone">Sierra Leone</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diffie_1-4"><a href="#cite_note-Diffie-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li>1470 – <a href="/wiki/Cape_Palmas" title="Cape Palmas">Cape Palmas</a> is passed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitfield_3-2"><a href="#cite_note-Whitfield-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li>1472 – <a href="/wiki/Fern%C3%A3o_do_P%C3%B3" title="Fernão do Pó">Fernão do Pó</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Bioko" title="Bioko">Bioko</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ravenstein_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-Ravenstein-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li>1473 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lopo_Gon%C3%A7alves" title="Lopo Gonçalves">Lopo Gonçalves</a> is the first to cross the <a href="/wiki/Equator" title="Equator">equator</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitfield_3-3"><a href="#cite_note-Whitfield-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ravenstein_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-Ravenstein-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li>1474–75 – Ruy de Sequeira discovers <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe" title="São Tomé and Príncipe">São Tomé and Príncipe</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ravenstein_4-2"><a href="#cite_note-Ravenstein-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li>1482 – <a href="/wiki/Diogo_C%C3%A3o" title="Diogo Cão">Diogo Cão</a> reaches the <a href="/wiki/Congo_River" title="Congo River">Congo River</a>, where he erects a "padrão" (pillar of stone).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ravenstein_4-3"><a href="#cite_note-Ravenstein-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li>1485–86 – Cão reaches <a href="/wiki/Cape_Cross" title="Cape Cross">Cape Cross</a>, where he erects his last padrão.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ravenstein_4-4"><a href="#cite_note-Ravenstein-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li>1487–92 – <a href="/wiki/P%C3%AAro_da_Covilh%C3%A3" title="Pêro da Covilhã">Pêro da Covilhã</a> travels to Arabia, down to the mouth of the Red Sea, eastward by sail to the <a href="/wiki/Malabar_Coast" title="Malabar Coast">Malabar Coast</a> (visiting <a href="/wiki/Kozhikode" title="Kozhikode">Calicut</a> and <a href="/wiki/Goa" title="Goa">Goa</a>); later sails down the east coast of Africa (visiting the trading stations of <a href="/wiki/Mombasa" title="Mombasa">Mombasa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zanzibar" title="Zanzibar">Zanzibar</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Sofala" title="Sofala">Sofala</a>); on his return he visits <a href="/wiki/Mecca" title="Mecca">Mecca</a> and <a href="/wiki/Medina" title="Medina">Medina</a> before reaching <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> in search of the mythical <a href="/wiki/Prester_John" title="Prester John">Prester John</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fleming2004_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fleming2004-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li>1488 – <a href="/wiki/Bartolomeu_Dias" title="Bartolomeu Dias">Bartolomeu Dias</a> rounds the "Cape of Storms" (<a href="/wiki/Cape_of_Good_Hope" title="Cape of Good Hope">Cape of Good Hope</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ravenstein_4-5"><a href="#cite_note-Ravenstein-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li>1492 – <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Columbus" title="Christopher Columbus">Christopher Columbus</a> discovers the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">Bahamas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, and "Española" (<a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">Hispaniola</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Taviani_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-Taviani-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li>1493–94 – Columbus discovers <a href="/wiki/Dominica" title="Dominica">Dominica</a> and <a href="/wiki/Guadeloupe" title="Guadeloupe">Guadeloupe</a>, among other islands of the <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">Lesser Antilles</a>; also discovers <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jamaica" title="Jamaica">Jamaica</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Taviani_6-1"><a href="#cite_note-Taviani-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li>1497 – <a href="/wiki/John_Cabot" title="John Cabot">John Cabot</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Newfoundland_(island)" title="Newfoundland (island)">Newfoundland</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>1497–98 – <a href="/wiki/Vasco_da_Gama" title="Vasco da Gama">Vasco da Gama</a> sails to <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> and back.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitfield_3-4"><a href="#cite_note-Whitfield-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li>1498 – Columbus discovers the mainland of <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">South America</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Taviani_6-2"><a href="#cite_note-Taviani-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li>1499 – <a href="/wiki/Alonso_de_Ojeda" title="Alonso de Ojeda">Alonso de Ojeda</a> explores the South American mainland from about <a href="/wiki/Cayenne" title="Cayenne">Cayenne</a> (in modern <a href="/wiki/French_Guiana" title="French Guiana">French Guiana</a>) to <a href="/wiki/Cabo_de_la_Vela" title="Cabo de la Vela">Cabo de la Vela</a> (in modern <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>), discovering the mouths of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orinoco_River" title="Orinoco River">Orinoco</a> and entering <a href="/wiki/Lake_Maracaibo" title="Lake Maracaibo">Lake Maracaibo</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1499 – <a href="/wiki/Amerigo_Vespucci" title="Amerigo Vespucci">Amerigo Vespucci</a> discovers the mouth of the <a href="/wiki/Amazon_River" title="Amazon River">Amazon River</a> and reaches 6°S, in present-day northern <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Pohl1966_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-Pohl1966-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li>1499 – <a href="/wiki/Jo%C3%A3o_Fernandes_Lavrador" title="João Fernandes Lavrador">João Fernandes <i>Lavrador</i></a>, together with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/P%C3%AAro_de_Barcelos" title="Pêro de Barcelos">Pêro de Barcelos</a>, sight <a href="/wiki/Labrador" title="Labrador">Labrador</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li>1499 – <a href="/wiki/Gaspar_Corte-Real" title="Gaspar Corte-Real">Gaspar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Miguel_Corte-Real" title="Miguel Corte-Real">Miguel Corte-Real</a> reach and map <a href="/wiki/Greenland" title="Greenland">Greenland</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-10">[10]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="16th_century">16th century</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_European_exploration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 16th century">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nau_de_Pedro_%C3%81lvares_Cabral.jpg"><img alt="An old painting depicting a wooden sailing ship with sails full blown by the wind" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="499" data-file-width="600" decoding="async" height="183" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Nau_de_Pedro_%C3%81lvares_Cabral.jpg/220px-Nau_de_Pedro_%C3%81lvares_Cabral.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Nau_de_Pedro_%C3%81lvares_Cabral.jpg/330px-Nau_de_Pedro_%C3%81lvares_Cabral.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Nau_de_Pedro_%C3%81lvares_Cabral.jpg/440px-Nau_de_Pedro_%C3%81lvares_Cabral.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Nau_de_Pedro_%C3%81lvares_Cabral.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cabral's ship on the fleet that sighted the Brazilian mainland for the first time on 22 April 1500. From the manuscript <i>Memória das Armadas que de Portugal passaram à Índia</i></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Balboa_s%C3%BCdsee.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="653" data-file-width="440" decoding="async" height="327" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/Balboa_s%C3%BCdsee.jpg/220px-Balboa_s%C3%BCdsee.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/Balboa_s%C3%BCdsee.jpg/330px-Balboa_s%C3%BCdsee.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/66/Balboa_s%C3%BCdsee.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Balboa_s%C3%BCdsee.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Balboa claiming possession of the Mar del Sur ("South Sea").</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tenochtitlan_y_Golfo_de_Mexico_1524.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1010" data-file-width="1600" decoding="async" height="158" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Tenochtitlan_y_Golfo_de_Mexico_1524.jpg/250px-Tenochtitlan_y_Golfo_de_Mexico_1524.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Tenochtitlan_y_Golfo_de_Mexico_1524.jpg/375px-Tenochtitlan_y_Golfo_de_Mexico_1524.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Tenochtitlan_y_Golfo_de_Mexico_1524.jpg/500px-Tenochtitlan_y_Golfo_de_Mexico_1524.jpg 2x" width="250"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Tenochtitlan_y_Golfo_de_Mexico_1524.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map of the island city <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tenochtitl%C3%A1n" title="Tenochtitlán">Tenochtitlán</a> and Mexico gulf made by one of Cortés' men, 1524, <a href="/wiki/Newberry_Library" title="Newberry Library">Newberry Library</a>, Chicago</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Discovery_of_the_Mississippi.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1948" data-file-width="3000" decoding="async" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Discovery_of_the_Mississippi.jpg/220px-Discovery_of_the_Mississippi.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Discovery_of_the_Mississippi.jpg/330px-Discovery_of_the_Mississippi.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Discovery_of_the_Mississippi.jpg/440px-Discovery_of_the_Mississippi.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Discovery_of_the_Mississippi.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i>Discovery of the Mississippi</i> by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/William_H._Powell" title="William H. Powell">William H. Powell</a> (1823–1879) is a <a href="/wiki/Romanticism" title="Romanticism">Romantic</a> depiction of de Soto seeing the Mississippi River for the first time. It hangs in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Capitol_rotunda" title="United States Capitol rotunda">United States Capitol rotunda</a>.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Coronado-Remington.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="768" decoding="async" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Coronado-Remington.jpg/220px-Coronado-Remington.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Coronado-Remington.jpg/330px-Coronado-Remington.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Coronado-Remington.jpg/440px-Coronado-Remington.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Coronado-Remington.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Coronado Sets Out to the North, by <a href="/wiki/Frederic_Remington" title="Frederic Remington">Frederic Remington</a>, 1861–1909</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Cabrillo_National_Monument_(Loki30).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1600" data-file-width="1200" decoding="async" height="293" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Cabrillo_National_Monument_%28Loki30%29.jpg/220px-Cabrillo_National_Monument_%28Loki30%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Cabrillo_National_Monument_%28Loki30%29.jpg/330px-Cabrillo_National_Monument_%28Loki30%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Cabrillo_National_Monument_%28Loki30%29.jpg/440px-Cabrillo_National_Monument_%28Loki30%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Cabrillo_National_Monument_(Loki30).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Cabrillo_National_Monument" title="Cabrillo National Monument">Cabrillo National Monument</a> in San Diego, California</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Polar_bear,_Gerrit_de_Veer_(1596).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="439" data-file-width="547" decoding="async" height="177" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Polar_bear%2C_Gerrit_de_Veer_%281596%29.jpg/220px-Polar_bear%2C_Gerrit_de_Veer_%281596%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Polar_bear%2C_Gerrit_de_Veer_%281596%29.jpg/330px-Polar_bear%2C_Gerrit_de_Veer_%281596%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Polar_bear%2C_Gerrit_de_Veer_%281596%29.jpg/440px-Polar_bear%2C_Gerrit_de_Veer_%281596%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Polar_bear,_Gerrit_de_Veer_(1596).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Crew of <a href="/wiki/Willem_Barentsz" title="Willem Barentsz">Willem Barentsz</a> fighting a <a href="/wiki/Polar_bear" title="Polar bear">polar bear</a>, 1596</div></div></div>
<ul><li>1500 – <a href="/wiki/Vicente_Y%C3%A1%C3%B1ez_Pinz%C3%B3n" title="Vicente Yáñez Pinzón">Vicente Yáñez Pinzón</a> reaches the northeast coast of what today is Brazil at a cape he names "Santa Maria de la Consolación" (<a href="/wiki/Cabo_de_Santo_Agostinho" title="Cabo de Santo Agostinho">Cabo de Santo Agostinho</a>) and sails fifty miles up a river he names the "Marañón" (<a href="/wiki/Amazon_River" title="Amazon River">Amazon</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-2"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1500 – <a href="/wiki/Pedro_%C3%81lvares_Cabral" title="Pedro Álvares Cabral">Pedro Álvares Cabral</a> makes the "official" discovery of Brazil,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-3"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup> leading the first <a href="/wiki/2nd_Portuguese_India_Armada_(Cabral,_1500)" title="2nd Portuguese India Armada (Cabral, 1500)">expedition</a> that united Europe, America, Africa, and Asia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li>1500 – <a href="/wiki/Jo%C3%A3o_Fernandes_Lavrador" title="João Fernandes Lavrador">João Fernandes</a> reaches <a href="/wiki/Cape_Farewell,_Greenland" title="Cape Farewell, Greenland">Cape Farewell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Greenland" title="Greenland">Greenland</a> ("Terra do Lavrador", or Land of the Husbandman).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-1"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>1500–02 – Gaspar and Miguel Corte Real discover and name the coasts of "Terra Verde" (likely Newfoundland) and Labrador.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-2"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_10-1"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li>1500-01 – <a href="/wiki/Diogo_Dias" title="Diogo Dias">Diogo Dias</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascar</a> and reaches the gate of the <a href="/wiki/Red_Sea" title="Red Sea">Red Sea</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Bab-el-Mandeb" title="Bab-el-Mandeb">Bab-el-Mandeb</a> Strait.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-4"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1500 – <a href="/wiki/Rodrigo_de_Bastidas" title="Rodrigo de Bastidas">Rodrigo de Bastidas</a> explores the Colombian coast from Cabo de la Vela to the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Urab%C3%A1" title="Gulf of Urabá">Gulf of Urabá</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-5"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1501-02 – <a href="/wiki/Gon%C3%A7alo_Coelho" title="Gonçalo Coelho">Gonçalo Coelho</a> discovers "Rio de Janeiro" (<a href="/wiki/Guanabara_Bay" title="Guanabara Bay">Guanabara Bay</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-6"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1502–03 – Columbus explores the <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North American</a> mainland from <a href="/wiki/Guanaja" title="Guanaja">Guanaja</a> off modern <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduras</a> to the present-day border of <a href="/wiki/Panama" title="Panama">Panama</a> and <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-7"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Taviani_6-3"><a href="#cite_note-Taviani-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li>1505 – <a href="/wiki/Juan_de_Berm%C3%BAdez" title="Juan de Bermúdez">Juan de Bermúdez</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">Bermuda</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-8"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1506 – <a href="/wiki/Louren%C3%A7o_de_Almeida" title="Lourenço de Almeida">Lourenço de Almeida</a> reaches the <a href="/wiki/Maldives" title="Maldives">Maldives</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></li>
<li>1506 – <a href="/wiki/Trist%C3%A3o_da_Cunha" title="Tristão da Cunha">Tristão da Cunha</a> discovers the island of <a href="/wiki/Tristan_da_Cunha" title="Tristan da Cunha">Tristan da Cunha</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li>1509 – <a href="/wiki/Diogo_Lopes_de_Sequeira" title="Diogo Lopes de Sequeira">Diogo Lopes de Sequeira</a> reaches <a href="/wiki/Sumatra" title="Sumatra">Sumatra</a> and <a href="/wiki/Malacca" title="Malacca">Malacca</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Marsden_14-0"><a href="#cite_note-Marsden-14">[14]</a></sup></li>
<li>1511 – <a href="/wiki/Duarte_Fernandes" title="Duarte Fernandes">Duarte Fernandes</a> leads a diplomatic mission to <a href="/wiki/Ayutthaya_Kingdom" title="Ayutthaya Kingdom">Ayutthaya Kingdom</a> (Siam or <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lach_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-Lach-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li>1511 – Rui Nunes da Cunha leads a diplomatic mission to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pegu" title="Pegu">Pegu</a> (Burma or <a href="/wiki/Myanmar" title="Myanmar">Myanmar</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lach_15-1"><a href="#cite_note-Lach-15">[15]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Galvano_16-0"><a href="#cite_note-Galvano-16">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li>1511–12 – <a href="/wiki/Jo%C3%A3o_de_Lisboa" title="João de Lisboa">João de Lisboa</a> and Estevão de Fróis discover the "Cape of Santa Maria" (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Punta_Del_Este" title="Punta Del Este">Punta Del Este</a>) in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rio_de_La_Plata" title="Rio de La Plata">River Plate</a>, exploring its estuary, and traveling as far south as the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gulf_of_San_Matias" title="Gulf of San Matias">Gulf of San Matias</a> at 42ºS, in present-day <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a> and <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> (penetrating 300 km (186 mi) "around the Gulf").<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li>1511–12 – <a href="/wiki/Ant%C3%B3nio_de_Abreu" title="António de Abreu">António de Abreu</a> sails through the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Malacca" title="Strait of Malacca">Strait of Malacca</a>, between Sumatra and <a href="/wiki/Bangka_Island" title="Bangka Island">Bangka</a>, and along the coasts of <a href="/wiki/Java" title="Java">Java</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bali" title="Bali">Bali</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lombok" title="Lombok">Lombok</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sumbawa" title="Sumbawa">Sumbawa</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Flores" title="Flores">Flores</a> to the "Spice Islands" (<a href="/wiki/Maluku_Islands" title="Maluku Islands">Maluku</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li>1513 – <a href="/wiki/Jorge_%C3%81lvares" title="Jorge Álvares">Jorge Álvares</a> lands off the coast of <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>, on <a href="/wiki/Nei_Lingding_Island" title="Nei Lingding Island">Nei Lingding Island</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Pearl_River_Delta" title="Pearl River Delta">Pearl River Delta</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diffie_1-5"><a href="#cite_note-Diffie-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li>1513 – <a href="/wiki/Vasco_N%C3%BA%C3%B1ez_de_Balboa" title="Vasco Núñez de Balboa">Vasco Núñez de Balboa</a> crosses the <a href="/wiki/Isthmus_of_Panama" title="Isthmus of Panama">Isthmus of Panama</a> and reaches the <a href="/wiki/Bay_of_San_Miguel" title="Bay of San Miguel">Bay of San Miguel</a>, discovering the "Mar del Sur" (<a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-9"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1513 – <a href="/wiki/Juan_Ponce_de_Le%C3%B3n" title="Juan Ponce de León">Juan Ponce de León</a> discovers "La Florida" (<a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a>) and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yucatan_Peninsula" title="Yucatan Peninsula">Yucatan</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-10"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1514–15 – António Fernandes reaches present-day <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Russell-Wood_20-0"><a href="#cite_note-Russell-Wood-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li>1515 – Gonzalo de Badajoz crosses the Isthmus of Panama at the site of <a href="/wiki/Nombre_de_Dios,_Col%C3%B3n" title="Nombre de Dios, Colón">Nombre de Dios</a>, reaching as far as the interior of the <a href="/wiki/Azuero_Peninsula" title="Azuero Peninsula">Azuero Peninsula</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bancroft_21-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bancroft-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li>1516 – <a href="/wiki/Juan_D%C3%ADaz_de_Sol%C3%ADs" title="Juan Díaz de Solís">Juan Díaz de Solís</a> explores the River Plate estuary and names it "La Mar Dulce" ("The Fresh-Water Sea").<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-11"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1516 – Portuguese traders land in <a href="/wiki/Da_Nang" title="Da Nang">Da Nang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Champa" title="Champa">Champa</a>, naming it <a href="/wiki/Cochinchina" title="Cochinchina">Cochinchina</a> (modern <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Li_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-Li-22">[22]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Yule_23-0"><a href="#cite_note-Yule-23">[23]</a></sup></li>
<li>1518 – Lourenço Gomes reaches <a href="/wiki/Borneo" title="Borneo">Borneo</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Keane_24-0"><a href="#cite_note-Keane-24">[24]</a></sup></li>
<li>1518 – <a href="/wiki/Juan_de_Grijalva" title="Juan de Grijalva">Juan de Grijalva</a> explores the <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexican</a> coast from "Patouchan" (<a href="/wiki/Champot%C3%B3n,_Campeche" title="Champotón, Campeche">Champotón</a>) to just north of the <a href="/wiki/P%C3%A1nuco_River" title="Pánuco River">Pánuco River</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-12"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1519 – <a href="/wiki/Hern%C3%A1n_Cort%C3%A9s" title="Hernán Cortés">Hernán Cortés</a> travels from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Veracruz,_Veracruz" title="Veracruz, Veracruz">Villa Rica de la Vera Cruz</a> to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aztec" title="Aztec">Aztec</a> capital of <a href="/wiki/Tenochtitlan" title="Tenochtitlan">Tenochtitlan</a> on <a href="/wiki/Lake_Texcoco" title="Lake Texcoco">Lake Texcoco</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Marks_25-0"><a href="#cite_note-Marks-25">[25]</a></sup></li>
<li>1519 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alonzo_Alvarez_de_Pineda" title="Alonzo Alvarez de Pineda">Alonzo Alvarez de Pineda</a> sails around the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">Gulf of Mexico</a> to the Pánuco, proving its insularity; also discovers the "Father of Waters" (the <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_River" title="Mississippi River">Mississippi</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-13"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1519 – <a href="/wiki/Gaspar_de_Espinosa" title="Gaspar de Espinosa">Gaspar de Espinosa</a> sails west along the west coasts of modern <a href="/wiki/Panama" title="Panama">Panama</a> and <a href="/wiki/Costa_Rica" title="Costa Rica">Costa Rica</a> as far as the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Nicoya" title="Gulf of Nicoya">Gulf of Nicoya</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bancroft_21-1"><a href="#cite_note-Bancroft-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li>1519–22 – <a href="/wiki/Ferdinand_Magellan" title="Ferdinand Magellan">Ferdinand Magellan</a>'s expedition completes the first circumnavigation of the <a href="/wiki/Globe" title="Globe">globe</a>, exploring the coast of <a href="/wiki/Patagonia" title="Patagonia">Patagonia</a> and discovering and traversing the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Magellan" title="Strait of Magellan">Strait of Magellan</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bergreen_26-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bergreen-26">[26]</a></sup></li>
<li>1520–21 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jo%C3%A3o_Alvares_Fagundes" title="João Alvares Fagundes">João Alvares Fagundes</a> explores <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burgeo,_Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="Burgeo, Newfoundland and Labrador">Burgeo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Saint_Pierre_and_Miquelon" title="Saint Pierre and Miquelon">Saint Pierre and Miquelon</a> in Newfoundland, and <a href="/wiki/Nova_Scotia" title="Nova Scotia">Nova Scotia</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Francisco_de_Souza1570_28-0"><a href="#cite_note-Francisco_de_Souza1570-28">[28]</a></sup></li>
<li>1521 – Francisco Gordillo and Pedro de Quexos find the mouth of a river they name "Rio de San Juan Bautista" (perhaps <a href="/wiki/Winyah_Bay" title="Winyah Bay">Winyah Bay</a> at the mouth of the <a href="/wiki/Pee_Dee_River" title="Pee Dee River">Pee Dee River</a> in modern <a href="/wiki/South_Carolina" title="South Carolina">South Carolina</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hayes_29-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hayes-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li>1521 – <a href="/wiki/Crist%C3%B3v%C3%A3o_Jacques" title="Cristóvão Jacques">Cristóvão Jacques</a> explores the Plate River and discovers the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Parana_River" title="Parana River">Parana River</a>, entering it for about 23 leagues (around 140 km), to near the present city of <a href="/wiki/Rosario,_Santa_Fe" title="Rosario, Santa Fe">Rosario</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Johson/Silva_30-0"><a href="#cite_note-Johson/Silva-30">[30]</a></sup></li>
<li>1522 – <a href="/wiki/Gil_Gonz%C3%A1lez_D%C3%A1vila" title="Gil González Dávila">Gil González Dávila</a> explores inland from the Gulf of Nicoya, discovering <a href="/wiki/Lake_Nicaragua" title="Lake Nicaragua">Lake Nicaragua</a>, while his pilot <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Ni%C3%B1o" title="Andrés Niño">Andrés Niño</a> explores along the coast to the west, discovering the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Fonseca" title="Gulf of Fonseca">Gulf of Fonseca</a> and perhaps reaching as far as the southwestern coast of modern <a href="/wiki/Guatemala" title="Guatemala">Guatemala</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bancroft_21-2"><a href="#cite_note-Bancroft-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li>1524 – <a href="/wiki/Giovanni_da_Verrazzano" title="Giovanni da Verrazzano">Giovanni da Verrazzano</a> explores the eastern seaboard of the present <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> from about <a href="/wiki/Cape_Fear_(headland)" title="Cape Fear (headland)">Cape Fear</a> to <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">Maine</a>; discovers the mouth of the <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">Hudson River</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-3"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>c. 1524 – <a href="/wiki/Aleixo_Garcia" title="Aleixo Garcia">Aleixo Garcia</a> travels westward from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Santa_Catarina_(island)" title="Santa Catarina (island)">Santa Catarina</a>, across the <a href="/wiki/Paran%C3%A1_River" title="Paraná River">Paraná</a> (perhaps sighting <a href="/wiki/Iguazu_Falls" title="Iguazu Falls">Iguazu Falls</a>) to the <a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">Paraguay</a> near the site of <a href="/wiki/Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Asunción">Asunción</a>, then across the <a href="/wiki/Gran_Chaco" title="Gran Chaco">Gran Chaco</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Andes" title="Andes">Andes</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Inca_Empire" title="Inca Empire">Inca frontier</a>, somewhere between <a href="/wiki/Mizque" title="Mizque">Mizque</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tomina_Province" title="Tomina Province">Tomina</a> in modern <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Goodman_31-0"><a href="#cite_note-Goodman-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li>1524–25 – <a href="/wiki/Francisco_Pizarro" title="Francisco Pizarro">Francisco Pizarro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Diego_de_Almagro" title="Diego de Almagro">Diego de Almagro</a> explore from Punta Piña (7° 56’ N) on the southern coast of Panama to the <a href="/wiki/San_Juan_River_(Colombia)" title="San Juan River (Colombia)">San Juan River</a> (4° N), on the west coast of Colombia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Prescott_32-0"><a href="#cite_note-Prescott-32">[32]</a></sup></li>
<li>1525 – <a href="/wiki/Est%C3%AAv%C3%A3o_Gomes" title="Estêvão Gomes">Estêvão Gomes</a> probes <a href="/wiki/Penobscot_Bay" title="Penobscot Bay">Penobscot Bay</a>, <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">Maine</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hayes_29-1"><a href="#cite_note-Hayes-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li>1525 – The Portuguese reach "Celebes" (<a href="/wiki/Sulawesi" title="Sulawesi">Sulawesi</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup></li>
<li>1525 – Diogo da Rocha and <a href="/wiki/Gomes_de_Sequeira" title="Gomes de Sequeira">Gomes de Sequeira</a> discover the <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Islands" title="Caroline Islands">Caroline Islands</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup></li>
<li>1526 – <a href="/wiki/Alonso_de_Salazar" title="Alonso de Salazar">Alonso de Salazar</a> discovers the <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands" title="Marshall Islands">Marshall Islands</a> (<a href="/wiki/Bokak_Atoll" title="Bokak Atoll">Bokak Atoll</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Quanchi_35-0"><a href="#cite_note-Quanchi-35">[35]</a></sup></li>
<li>1526–28 – Pizarro and his pilot Bartolomé Ruiz explore the west coast of South America from the San Juan River south to the <a href="/wiki/Santa_River" title="Santa River">Santa River</a> (about 9° S), becoming the first to sight the coasts of <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a> and <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Prescott_32-1"><a href="#cite_note-Prescott-32">[32]</a></sup></li>
<li>1526–27 – <a href="/wiki/Jorge_de_Menezes" title="Jorge de Menezes">Jorge de Menezes</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/New_Guinea" title="New Guinea">New Guinea</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whiteway_36-0"><a href="#cite_note-Whiteway-36">[36]</a></sup></li>
<li>1527–28 – <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Cabot_(explorer)" title="Sebastian Cabot (explorer)">Sebastian Cabot</a> explores several hundred miles up the Paraná River, past its confluence with the Paraguay.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-14"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1528 – <a href="/wiki/Diogo_Rodrigues" title="Diogo Rodrigues">Diogo Rodrigues</a> explores the <a href="/wiki/Mascarene_Islands" title="Mascarene Islands">Mascarene Islands</a> (which he names after <a href="/wiki/Pedro_Mascarenhas" title="Pedro Mascarenhas">Pedro Mascarenhas</a>), naming the islands of <a href="/wiki/R%C3%A9union" title="Réunion">Réunion</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mauritius" title="Mauritius">Mauritius</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rodrigues_(island)" title="Rodrigues (island)">Rodrigues</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fonseca_37-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fonseca-37">[37]</a></sup></li>
<li>1528–36 – <a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvar_N%C3%BA%C3%B1ez_Cabeza_de_Vaca" title="Álvar Núñez Cabeza de Vaca">Álvar Núñez Cabeza de Vaca</a> and three others are the only survivors of a group of several hundred colonists who travel from the coast of western Florida to the Rio Sinaloa in northern Mexico, where they encounter <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spanish</a> <a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">slavers</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Reséndez_38-0"><a href="#cite_note-Reséndez-38">[38]</a></sup></li>
<li>1531 – <a href="/wiki/Diego_de_Ordaz" title="Diego de Ordaz">Diego de Ordaz</a> ascends the Orinoco to the Atures rapids, just past its confluence with the <a href="/wiki/Meta_River" title="Meta River">Meta</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Goodman_31-1"><a href="#cite_note-Goodman-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li>1532–33 – Pizarro explores and conquers inland to <a href="/wiki/Cajamarca" title="Cajamarca">Cajamarca</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cuzco" title="Cuzco">Cuzco</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Goodman_31-2"><a href="#cite_note-Goodman-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li>1533 – <a href="/wiki/Fort%C3%BAn_Xim%C3%A9nez" title="Fortún Ximénez">Fortún Ximénez</a> finds the tip of <a href="/wiki/Baja_California" title="Baja California">Baja California</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hayes2007_39-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hayes2007-39">[39]</a></sup></li>
<li>1534 – <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Cartier" title="Jacques Cartier">Jacques Cartier</a> explores the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gulf_of_St._Lawrence" title="Gulf of St. Lawrence">Gulf of St. Lawrence</a>, discovering <a href="/wiki/Anticosti_Island" title="Anticosti Island">Anticosti Island</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prince_Edward_Island" title="Prince Edward Island">Prince Edward Island</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-4"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>1535 – <a href="/wiki/Fray_Tom%C3%A1s_de_Berlanga" title="Fray Tomás de Berlanga">Fray Tomás de Berlanga</a> discovers the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Galapagos_Islands" title="Galapagos Islands">Galapagos Islands</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup></li>
<li>1535 – Cartier ascends "La Grande Rivière" or "La Rivière de Hochelaga" (the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Lawrence_River" title="St. Lawrence River">St. Lawrence River</a>) to the village of <a href="/wiki/Hochelaga_(village)" title="Hochelaga (village)">Hochelaga</a> (present-day <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">Montreal</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-5"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>1535–37 – Diego de Almagro leads en expedition from Cuzco to the south, taking the <a href="/wiki/Inca_road_system" title="Inca road system">Inca highway</a> to the southwest shore of <a href="/wiki/Lake_Titicaca" title="Lake Titicaca">Lake Titicaca</a>, through the <a href="/wiki/Altiplano" title="Altiplano">altiplano</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Salta_Province" title="Salta Province">Salta valley</a> to <a href="/wiki/Copiap%C3%B3_Province" title="Copiapó Province">Copiapó</a>; a detachment continues south to the <a href="/wiki/Maule_River" title="Maule River">Maule River</a>. Almagro takes the coastal route back, through the <a href="/wiki/Atacama_Desert" title="Atacama Desert">Atacama Desert</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Goodman_31-3"><a href="#cite_note-Goodman-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li>1539 – <a href="/wiki/Francisco_de_Ulloa" title="Francisco de Ulloa">Francisco de Ulloa</a> sails to the head of the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_California" title="Gulf of California">Gulf of California</a> and around Baja California to <a href="/wiki/Cedros_Island" title="Cedros Island">Cedros Island</a>, establishing that Baja is a peninsula.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hayes2007_39-1"><a href="#cite_note-Hayes2007-39">[39]</a></sup></li>
<li>1539–43 – <a href="/wiki/Hernando_de_Soto" title="Hernando de Soto">Hernando de Soto</a>'s expedition explores much of the modern <a href="/wiki/Southern_United_States" title="Southern United States">American South</a>, becoming the first to cross the <a href="/wiki/Appalachian_Mountains" title="Appalachian Mountains">Appalachians</a> (over the <a href="/wiki/Blue_Ridge_Mountain" title="Blue Ridge Mountain">Blue Ridge Mountains</a>) and the Mississippi.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-15"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hayes_29-2"><a href="#cite_note-Hayes-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li>1540–42 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Francisco_V%C3%A1squez_de_Coronado" title="Francisco Vásquez de Coronado">Francisco Vásquez de Coronado</a> searches for the mythical <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Seven_Cities_of_Cibola" title="Seven Cities of Cibola">Seven Cities of Cibola</a>, only to find <a href="/wiki/Zuni-Cibola_Complex" title="Zuni-Cibola Complex">villages of mud and thatch</a>. He sends out smaller parties, one of which, under <a href="/wiki/Garc%C3%ADa_L%C3%B3pez_de_C%C3%A1rdenas" title="García López de Cárdenas">García López de Cárdenas</a>, discovers the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Canyon" title="Grand Canyon">Grand Canyon</a>; another finds a city of <a href="/wiki/Gold" title="Gold">gold</a> called <a href="/wiki/Quivira" title="Quivira">Quivira</a> (in modern <a href="/wiki/Kansas" title="Kansas">Kansas</a>), which Coronado later visits — although he finds no gold.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hayes_29-3"><a href="#cite_note-Hayes-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li>1540 – <a href="/wiki/Hernando_de_Alarc%C3%B3n" title="Hernando de Alarcón">Hernando de Alarcón</a> ascends the <a href="/wiki/Colorado_River" title="Colorado River">Colorado River</a> to the confluence of the <a href="/wiki/Gila_River" title="Gila River">Gila River</a> (near present-day <a href="/wiki/Yuma,_Arizona" title="Yuma, Arizona">Yuma, Arizona</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hayes2007_39-2"><a href="#cite_note-Hayes2007-39">[39]</a></sup></li>
<li>1541–42 – <a href="/wiki/Francisco_de_Orellana" title="Francisco de Orellana">Francisco de Orellana</a> sails down the length of the Amazon.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Smith_41-0"><a href="#cite_note-Smith-41">[41]</a></sup></li>
<li>1542–43 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Juan_Rodriguez_Cabrillo" title="Juan Rodriguez Cabrillo">Juan Rodriguez Cabrillo</a> explores the coasts of modern Baja and <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> from Punta Baja to the <a href="/wiki/Russian_River_(California)" title="Russian River (California)">Russian River</a>, discovering the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Channel_Islands_of_California" title="Channel Islands of California">Channel Islands</a>; after his death, his second-in-command, <a href="/wiki/Bartolom%C3%A9_Ferrer" title="Bartolomé Ferrer">Bartolomé Ferrer</a>, reaches <a href="/wiki/Point_Arena,_California" title="Point Arena, California">Point Arena</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kelsey_42-0"><a href="#cite_note-Kelsey-42">[42]</a></sup></li>
<li>1542 or 1543 – <a href="/wiki/Fern%C3%A3o_Mendes_Pinto" title="Fernão Mendes Pinto">Fernão Mendes Pinto</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ant%C3%B3nio_Mota" title="António Mota">António Mota</a> and Francisco Zeimoto reach <a href="/wiki/Tanegashima" title="Tanegashima">Tanegashima</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diffie_1-6"><a href="#cite_note-Diffie-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li>1543 – <a href="/wiki/Ruy_L%C3%B3pez_de_Villalobos" title="Ruy López de Villalobos">Ruy López de Villalobos</a> discovers three islands (<a href="/wiki/Fais_Island" title="Fais Island">Fais</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ulithi" title="Ulithi">Ulithi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yap" title="Yap">Yap</a>) in the <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Islands" title="Caroline Islands">Carolines</a> and eight atolls (<a href="/wiki/Kwajalein_Atoll" title="Kwajalein Atoll">Kwajalein</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lae_Atoll" title="Lae Atoll">Lae</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ujae_Atoll" title="Ujae Atoll">Ujae</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wotho_Atoll" title="Wotho Atoll">Wotho</a>, <a href="/wiki/Likiep_Atoll" title="Likiep Atoll">Likiep</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wotje_Atoll" title="Wotje Atoll">Wotje</a>, <a href="/wiki/Erikub_Atoll" title="Erikub Atoll">Erikub</a> and <a href="/wiki/Maloelap_Atoll" title="Maloelap Atoll">Maloelap</a>) in the Marshall Islands.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Quanchi_35-1"><a href="#cite_note-Quanchi-35">[35]</a></sup></li>
<li>1543 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jean_Alfonce" title="Jean Alfonce">Jean Alfonce</a> explores up the <a href="/wiki/Saguenay_River" title="Saguenay River">Saguenay River</a>, believing it to be "la mer du Cattay".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-6"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>1553 – <a href="/wiki/Hugh_Willoughby" title="Hugh Willoughby">Hugh Willoughby</a> seeks a <a href="/wiki/Northeast_Passage" title="Northeast Passage">Northeast Passage</a> over <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>; reaches either <a href="/wiki/Kolguyev_Island" title="Kolguyev Island">Kolguyev Island</a> or <a href="/wiki/Novaya_Zemlya" title="Novaya Zemlya">Novaya Zemlya</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vaughan_43-0"><a href="#cite_note-Vaughan-43">[43]</a></sup></li>
<li>1556 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Steven_Borough" title="Steven Borough">Steven Borough</a> reaches as far as <a href="/wiki/Kara_Strait" title="Kara Strait">Kara Strait</a>, between Novaya Zemlya and <a href="/wiki/Vaygach_Island" title="Vaygach Island">Vaygach Island</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vaughan_43-1"><a href="#cite_note-Vaughan-43">[43]</a></sup></li>
<li>1557–59 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Juan_Fern%C3%A1ndez_Ladrillero" title="Juan Fernández Ladrillero">Juan Fernández Ladrillero</a> and Cortés Hojea explore the <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chilean</a> coast from <a href="/wiki/Valdivia" title="Valdivia">Valdivia</a> (39° 48’ S) to Canal Santa Barbara (54° S); the former passes through the western entrance of the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Magellan" title="Strait of Magellan">Strait of Magellan</a> to its eastern entrance and back.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-16"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li>1565 – <a href="/wiki/Miguel_L%C3%B3pez_de_Legazpi" title="Miguel López de Legazpi">Miguel López de Legazpi</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Mejit_Island" title="Mejit Island">Mejit</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ailuk_Atoll" title="Ailuk Atoll">Ailuk</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jemo_Island" title="Jemo Island">Jemo</a> in the Marshall Islands, while his subordinate <a href="/wiki/Alonso_de_Arellano" title="Alonso de Arellano">Alonso de Arellano</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Lib_Island" title="Lib Island">Lib</a> in the same island group, as well as five islands (<a href="/wiki/Oroluk_Atoll" title="Oroluk Atoll">Oroluk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chuuk_State" title="Chuuk State">Chuuk</a>, Pulap, <a href="/wiki/Sorol" title="Sorol">Sorol</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ngulu_Atoll" title="Ngulu Atoll">Ngulu</a>) in the Caroline Islands.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Quanchi_35-2"><a href="#cite_note-Quanchi-35">[35]</a></sup></li>
<li>1568 – <a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvaro_de_Menda%C3%B1a_de_Neira" title="Álvaro de Mendaña de Neira">Álvaro de Mendaña</a> discovers the <a href="/wiki/Solomon_Islands" title="Solomon Islands">Solomon Islands</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitfield_3-5"><a href="#cite_note-Whitfield-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li>1576 – <a href="/wiki/Martin_Frobisher" title="Martin Frobisher">Martin Frobisher</a> discovers "Meta Incognita" ("the unknown bourne"; <a href="/wiki/Baffin_Island" title="Baffin Island">Baffin Island</a>) and what he believes to be a passage to Cathay: "Frobishers Streytes" (<a href="/wiki/Frobisher_Bay" title="Frobisher Bay">Frobisher Bay</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-7"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>1577–80 – <a href="/wiki/Francis_Drake" title="Francis Drake">Sir Francis Drake</a> completes the second circumnavigation of the globe.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bawlf_44-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bawlf-44">[44]</a></sup></li>
<li>1578 – Frobisher sails part way up the "Mistaken Straites" (<a href="/wiki/Hudson_Strait" title="Hudson Strait">Hudson Strait</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-8"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>1581–82 – <a href="/wiki/Yermak_Timofeyevich" title="Yermak Timofeyevich">Yermak Timofeyevich</a> and his men cross the <a href="/wiki/Ural_Mountains" title="Ural Mountains">Ural Mountains</a> and reach as far as <a href="/wiki/Qashliq" title="Qashliq">Isker</a> on the banks of the <a href="/wiki/Irtysh_River" title="Irtysh River">Irtysh</a> (near modern <a href="/wiki/Tobolsk" title="Tobolsk">Tobolsk</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lincoln_45-0"><a href="#cite_note-Lincoln-45">[45]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lantzeff_46-0"><a href="#cite_note-Lantzeff-46">[46]</a></sup></li>
<li>1585 – <a href="/wiki/John_Davis_(English_explorer)" title="John Davis (English explorer)">John Davis</a> explores <a href="/wiki/Davis_Strait" title="Davis Strait">Davis Strait</a>, reaching 66°40′ N; also sails up <a href="/wiki/Cumberland_Sound" title="Cumberland Sound">Cumberland Sound</a>, thinking it to be a "passage to Cathay".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-9"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>1587 – Davis sails up the west coast of <a href="/wiki/Greenland" title="Greenland">Greenland</a> as far as 72°46′ N (about modern <a href="/wiki/Upernavik" title="Upernavik">Upernavik</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison_7-10"><a href="#cite_note-Morison-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>1589 – <a href="/wiki/Jo%C3%A3o_da_Gama" title="João da Gama">João da Gama</a> reaches "Yezo" (<a href="/wiki/Hokkaido" title="Hokkaido">Hokkaido</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup></li>
<li>1592 – Davis discovers the <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Markham1889_48-0"><a href="#cite_note-Markham1889-48">[48]</a></sup></li>
<li>1595 – Mendaña discovers the <a href="/wiki/Marquesas_Islands" title="Marquesas Islands">Marquesas</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Whitfield_3-6"><a href="#cite_note-Whitfield-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li>1596 – <a href="/wiki/Willem_Barentsz" title="Willem Barentsz">Willem Barentsz</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Spitsbergen" title="Spitsbergen">Spitsbergen</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Conway_49-0"><a href="#cite_note-Conway-49">[49]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="17th_century">17th century</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_European_exploration&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 17th century">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Last_Voyage_Of_Henry_Hudson.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="1292" decoding="async" height="262" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/Last_Voyage_Of_Henry_Hudson.jpg/220px-Last_Voyage_Of_Henry_Hudson.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/Last_Voyage_Of_Henry_Hudson.jpg/330px-Last_Voyage_Of_Henry_Hudson.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/Last_Voyage_Of_Henry_Hudson.jpg/440px-Last_Voyage_Of_Henry_Hudson.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Last_Voyage_Of_Henry_Hudson.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/John_Collier_(Pre-Raphaelite_painter)" title="John Collier (Pre-Raphaelite painter)">John Collier</a>'s painting of Henry Hudson cast adrift.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Krsk_koch.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2816" data-file-width="2112" decoding="async" height="293" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Krsk_koch.JPG/220px-Krsk_koch.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Krsk_koch.JPG/330px-Krsk_koch.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Krsk_koch.JPG/440px-Krsk_koch.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Krsk_koch.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A 17th-century <a href="/wiki/Koch_(boat)" title="Koch (boat)">koch</a> in a museum in <a href="/wiki/Krasnoyarsk" title="Krasnoyarsk">Krasnoyarsk</a>. Kochi were used to explore the <a href="/wiki/Siberia" title="Siberia">Siberian</a> watershed and coasts by men such as Kurochkin, Perfilyev and Dezhnev.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Gilsemans_1642.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1948" data-file-width="3000" decoding="async" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Gilsemans_1642.jpg/220px-Gilsemans_1642.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Gilsemans_1642.jpg/330px-Gilsemans_1642.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Gilsemans_1642.jpg/440px-Gilsemans_1642.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Gilsemans_1642.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>"Murderers' Bay", on the South Island of New Zealand, where several of Tasman's men were killed by Maori in December 1642.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%D0%9A%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%92._%D0%9B%D0%B5%D0%B1%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B5%D0%B2_-_%D0%AD%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%BF%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B8%D1%86%D0%B8%D1%8F_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%BC%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%94%D0%B5%D0%B6%D0%BD%D1%91%D0%B2%D0%B0.jpg"><img srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/%D0%9A%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%92._%D0%9B%D0%B5%D0%B1%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B5%D0%B2_-_%D0%AD%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%BF%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B8%D1%86%D0%B8%D1%8F_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%BC%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%94%D0%B5%D0%B6%D0%BD%D1%91%D0%B2%D0%B0.jpg/330px-%D0%9A%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%92._%D0%9B%D0%B5%D0%B1%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B5%D0%B2_-_%D0%AD%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%BF%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B8%D1%86%D0%B8%D1%8F_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%BC%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%94%D0%B5%D0%B6%D0%BD%D1%91%D0%B2%D0%B0.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/%D0%9A%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%92._%D0%9B%D0%B5%D0%B1%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B5%D0%B2_-_%D0%AD%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%BF%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B8%D1%86%D0%B8%D1%8F_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%BC%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%94%D0%B5%D0%B6%D0%BD%D1%91%D0%B2%D0%B0.jpg/440px-%D0%9A%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%92._%D0%9B%D0%B5%D0%B1%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B5%D0%B2_-_%D0%AD%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%BF%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B8%D1%86%D0%B8%D1%8F_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%BC%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%94%D0%B5%D0%B6%D0%BD%D1%91%D0%B2%D0%B0.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:%D0%9A%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%92._%D0%9B%D0%B5%D0%B1%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B5%D0%B2_-_%D0%AD%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%BF%D0%B5%D0%B4%D0%B8%D1%86%D0%B8%D1%8F_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%BC%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%94%D0%B5%D0%B6%D0%BD%D1%91%D0%B2%D0%B0.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i>The expedition of Semyon Dezhnyov</i> by <a href="/wiki/Klavdy_Lebedev" title="Klavdy Lebedev">Klavdy Lebedev</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pere_Marquette.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1686" data-file-width="2096" decoding="async" height="177" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Pere_Marquette.JPG/220px-Pere_Marquette.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Pere_Marquette.JPG/330px-Pere_Marquette.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Pere_Marquette.JPG/440px-Pere_Marquette.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pere_Marquette.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i>Pere Marquette and the Indians</i> at the Mississippi River, oil painting (1869) by <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Wilhelm_Lamprecht&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Wilhelm Lamprecht (page does not exist)">Wilhelm Lamprecht</a> (1838–1906), at <a href="/wiki/Marquette_University" title="Marquette University">Marquette University</a>.</div></div></div>
<ul><li>1600–01 – Prince Miron Shakhovskoi and D. Khripunov  descend the <a href="/wiki/Ob_River" title="Ob River">Ob</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Ob" title="Gulf of Ob">Ob Estuary</a> and ascend the <a href="/wiki/Taz_River" title="Taz River">Taz River</a>, establishing the <a href="/wiki/Ostrog_(fortress)" title="Ostrog (fortress)">ostrog</a> of <a href="/wiki/Mangazeya" title="Mangazeya">Mangazeya</a> about 161 kilometres (100 mi) to 240 kilometres (150 mi) from its mouth.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lantzeff_46-1"><a href="#cite_note-Lantzeff-46">[46]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Forsyth_50-0"><a href="#cite_note-Forsyth-50">[50]</a></sup></li>
<li>1602–06 – <a href="/wiki/Bento_de_G%C3%B3is" title="Bento de Góis">Bento de Góis</a> travels overland from India to China, via <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pamirs" title="Pamirs">Pamirs</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wessels_51-0"><a href="#cite_note-Wessels-51">[51]</a></sup></li>
<li>1605 – <a href="/wiki/Ket_River" title="Ket River">Ketsk</a> serving men ascend the <a href="/wiki/Ket_River" title="Ket River">Ket</a>, portage to the <a href="/wiki/Yenisei_River" title="Yenisei River">Yenisei</a>, and descend it to its confluence with the <a href="/wiki/Sym_River" title="Sym River">Sym</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fisher1943_52-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fisher1943-52">[52]</a></sup></li>
<li>1606 – <a href="/wiki/Willem_Janszoon" title="Willem Janszoon">Willem Janszoon</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> at the mouth of the <a href="/wiki/Pennefather_River" title="Pennefather River">Pennefather River</a> on the western coast of the <a href="/wiki/Cape_York_Peninsula" title="Cape York Peninsula">Cape York Peninsula</a>, exploring its coast from <a href="/wiki/Badu_Island" title="Badu Island">Badu Island</a> south to Cape Keerweer (13°58′ S).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mutch_53-0"><a href="#cite_note-Mutch-53">[53]</a></sup></li>
<li>1606 – <a href="/wiki/Pedro_Fernandes_de_Queir%C3%B3s" title="Pedro Fernandes de Queirós">Pedro Fernandes de Queirós</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Espiritu_Santo" title="Espiritu Santo">Espiritu Santo</a>, the largest island in what is now the nation of <a href="/wiki/Vanuatu" title="Vanuatu">Vanuatu</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mutch_53-1"><a href="#cite_note-Mutch-53">[53]</a></sup></li>
<li>1606 – <a href="/wiki/Lu%C3%ADs_Vaz_de_Torres" title="Luís Vaz de Torres">Luís Vaz de Torres</a> sails through <a href="/wiki/Torres_Strait" title="Torres Strait">the strait</a> that now bears his name.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mutch_53-2"><a href="#cite_note-Mutch-53">[53]</a></sup></li>
<li>1607 – Mangazeyan <i><a href="/wiki/Promyshlenniki" title="Promyshlenniki">promyshlenniki</a></i> and traders reach the lower <a href="/wiki/Yenisei_River" title="Yenisei River">Yenisei</a>, establish <a href="/wiki/Turukhansk" title="Turukhansk">Turukhansk</a>, and ascend the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nizhnyaya_Tunguska" title="Nizhnyaya Tunguska">Lower Tunguska</a>, while Ketsk serving men ascend the Yenisei to the <a href="/wiki/Angara_River" title="Angara River">Angara</a>, which they also ascend.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fisher1943_52-1"><a href="#cite_note-Fisher1943-52">[52]</a></sup></li>
<li>1607 – <a href="/wiki/Henry_Hudson" title="Henry Hudson">Henry Hudson</a> coasts the east coast of Greenland, naming "Hold-with-Hope" (around 73° N).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Asher_54-0"><a href="#cite_note-Asher-54">[54]</a></sup></li>
<li>1609 – Hudson sails the <i>Halve Maen</i> up the <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">Hudson River</a> as fall north as present day <a href="/wiki/Albany,_New_York" title="Albany, New York">Albany, New York</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hunter_55-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hunter-55">[55]</a></sup></li>
<li>1610 – <a href="/wiki/%C3%89tienne_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9" title="Étienne Brûlé">Étienne Brûlé</a> ascends the <a href="/wiki/Ottawa_River" title="Ottawa River">Ottawa River</a> and reaches <a href="/wiki/Lake_Nipissing" title="Lake Nipissing">Lake Nipissing</a> and <a href="/wiki/Georgian_Bay" title="Georgian Bay">Georgian Bay</a> in <a href="/wiki/Lake_Huron" title="Lake Huron">Lake Huron</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Butterfield_56-0"><a href="#cite_note-Butterfield-56">[56]</a></sup></li>
<li>1610 – Kondratiy Kurochkin leads an expedition, sailing in <a href="/wiki/Koch_(boat)" title="Koch (boat)">kochi</a>, from Turukhansk to the mouth of the <a href="/wiki/Yenisei_River" title="Yenisei River">Yenisei</a> and east to the mouth of the <a href="/wiki/Pyasina_River" title="Pyasina River">Pyasina</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Taymyr_Peninsula" title="Taymyr Peninsula">Taymyr Peninsula</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vaughan_43-2"><a href="#cite_note-Vaughan-43">[43]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lantzeff_46-2"><a href="#cite_note-Lantzeff-46">[46]</a></sup></li>
<li>1610 – A detachment from Mangazeya ascends the Yenisei a further 640 kilometres (400 mi) to its confluence with the <a href="/wiki/Sym_River" title="Sym River">Sym</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fisher1943_52-2"><a href="#cite_note-Fisher1943-52">[52]</a></sup></li>
<li>1610–11 – Hudson sails through <a href="/wiki/Hudson_Strait" title="Hudson Strait">Hudson Strait</a> into <a href="/wiki/Hudson_Bay" title="Hudson Bay">Hudson Bay</a>, where he overwinters in <a href="/wiki/James_Bay" title="James Bay">James Bay</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup></li>
<li>1611 – Mangazeyan men reach the <a href="/wiki/Khatanga_River" title="Khatanga River">Khatanga</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Armstrong2010_58-0"><a href="#cite_note-Armstrong2010-58">[58]</a></sup></li>
<li>1612–13 – <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Button" title="Thomas Button">Thomas Button</a> is the first to explore the western shores of <a href="/wiki/Hudson_Bay" title="Hudson Bay">Hudson Bay</a>, where he winters in the mouth of the <a href="/wiki/Nelson_River" title="Nelson River">Nelson River</a>; also discovers <a href="/wiki/Coats_Island" title="Coats Island">Coats</a> and <a href="/wiki/Southampton_Island" title="Southampton Island">Southampton Islands</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Christy_59-0"><a href="#cite_note-Christy-59">[59]</a></sup></li>
<li>1614 – <a href="/wiki/History_of_whaling" title="History of whaling">Whalers</a> discover <a href="/wiki/Jan_Mayen" title="Jan Mayen">Jan Mayen</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hacq_60-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hacq-60">[60]</a></sup></li>
<li>1615–16 – Étienne Brûlé sights the western shore of <a href="/wiki/Lake_Ontario" title="Lake Ontario">Lake Ontario</a>, descends the <a href="/wiki/Niagara_River" title="Niagara River">Niagara River</a>, explores what are now parts of modern <a href="/wiki/New_York_(state)" title="New York (state)">New York</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">Pennsylvania</a>, and descends the <a href="/wiki/Susquehanna_River" title="Susquehanna River">Susquehanna River</a> to <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">Chesapeake Bay</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Butterfield_56-1"><a href="#cite_note-Butterfield-56">[56]</a></sup></li>
<li>1616 – <a href="/wiki/Jacob_Le_Maire" title="Jacob Le Maire">Jacob Le Maire</a> and <a href="/wiki/Willem_Schouten" title="Willem Schouten">Willem Schouten</a> discover and name <a href="/wiki/Le_Maire_Strait" title="Le Maire Strait">Le Maire Strait</a>, <a href="/wiki/Isla_de_los_Estados" title="Isla de los Estados">Staten Island</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Cape_Horn" title="Cape Horn">Cape Horn</a>; also discover <a href="/wiki/Tonga" title="Tonga">Tonga</a> (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Niuafo%27ou" title="Niuafo'ou">Niuafo'ou</a>, <a href="/wiki/Niuatoputapu" title="Niuatoputapu">Niuatoputapu</a>, and  <a href="/wiki/Tafahi" title="Tafahi">Tafahi</a>), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Futuna_Island,_Wallis_and_Futuna" title="Futuna Island, Wallis and Futuna">Futuna</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alofi" title="Alofi">Alofi</a> (in modern <a href="/wiki/Wallis_and_Futuna" title="Wallis and Futuna">Wallis and Futuna</a>), and several islands in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tuamotu_Archipelago" title="Tuamotu Archipelago">Tuamotu</a> (<a href="/wiki/Takaroa" title="Takaroa">Takaroa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Takapoto" title="Takapoto">Takapoto</a>, <a href="/wiki/Manihi" title="Manihi">Manihi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ahe" title="Ahe">Ahe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rangiroa" title="Rangiroa">Rangiroa</a>)  and <a href="/wiki/Bismarck_Archipelago" title="Bismarck Archipelago">Bismarck Archipelagos</a> (including <a href="/wiki/New_Hanover_Island" title="New Hanover Island">New Hanover</a> and <a href="/wiki/New_Ireland_(island)" title="New Ireland (island)">New Ireland</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Morison1974_2-17"><a href="#cite_note-Morison1974-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Quanchi_35-3"><a href="#cite_note-Quanchi-35">[35]</a></sup></li>
<li>1616 – <a href="/wiki/Robert_Bylot" title="Robert Bylot">Robert Bylot</a> and <a href="/wiki/William_Baffin" title="William Baffin">William Baffin</a> reach 77°30′ N, enter <a href="/wiki/Baffin_Bay" title="Baffin Bay">Baffin Bay</a>, discover <a href="/wiki/Smith_Sound" title="Smith Sound">Smith</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jones_Sound" title="Jones Sound">Jones</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Lancaster_Sound" title="Lancaster Sound">Lancaster Sounds</a> and sight the coasts of <a href="/wiki/Ellesmere_Island" title="Ellesmere Island">Ellesmere</a>, <a href="/wiki/Devon_Island" title="Devon Island">Devon</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Bylot_Island" title="Bylot Island">Bylot Islands</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Markham_61-0"><a href="#cite_note-Markham-61">[61]</a></sup></li>
<li>1616 – <a href="/wiki/Dirk_Hartog" title="Dirk Hartog">Dirk Hartog</a> explores some 576 kilometres (358 mi) of coastline (the coast of <a href="/wiki/Western_Australia" title="Western Australia">Western Australia</a> from about 22° to 28° S), discovering <a href="/wiki/Dirk_Hartog_Island" title="Dirk Hartog Island">Dirk Hartog Island</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shark_Bay" title="Shark Bay">Shark Bay</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wood_62-0"><a href="#cite_note-Wood-62">[62]</a></sup></li>
<li>1617 – <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> <a href="/wiki/Walrus" title="Walrus">walrus</a> hunters sight the southern coast of "Sir Thomas Smith's Island" (<a href="/wiki/Nordaustlandet" title="Nordaustlandet">Nordaustlandet</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Conway_49-1"><a href="#cite_note-Conway-49">[49]</a></sup></li>
<li>1618 – <a href="/wiki/Pedro_P%C3%A1ez" title="Pedro Páez">Pedro Páez</a> is believed to be the first European to see and describe the source of the <a href="/wiki/Blue_Nile" title="Blue Nile">Blue Nile</a> in Ethiopia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Budge_63-0"><a href="#cite_note-Budge-63">[63]</a></sup></li>
<li>1618 – <a href="/wiki/Lenaert_Jacobszoon" title="Lenaert Jacobszoon">Lenaert Jacobszoon</a> discovers an "island" at 22° S (the coast of Western Australia from <a href="/wiki/Point_Cloates" title="Point Cloates">Point Cloates</a> to <a href="/wiki/North_West_Cape" title="North West Cape">North West Cape</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mutch_53-3"><a href="#cite_note-Mutch-53">[53]</a></sup></li>
<li>1619 – <a href="/wiki/Frederick_de_Houtman" title="Frederick de Houtman">Frederick de Houtman</a> sights the coast of Western Australia near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fremantle,_Western_Australia" title="Fremantle, Western Australia">Fremantle</a> and sails along the coast north for over 640 kilometres (400 mi).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mutch_53-4"><a href="#cite_note-Mutch-53">[53]</a></sup></li>
<li>1620 – Mangazeyan serving men reach the <a href="/wiki/Vilyuy_River" title="Vilyuy River">Vilyuy River</a> and descend it to its confluence with the <a href="/wiki/Lena_River" title="Lena River">Lena</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fisher1943_52-3"><a href="#cite_note-Fisher1943-52">[52]</a></sup></li>
<li>1621–23 – Étienne Brûlé and his companion Grenolle travel along the <a href="/wiki/North_Channel_(Ontario)" title="North Channel (Ontario)">North Channel</a> of Lake Huron (probably sighting <a href="/wiki/Manitoulin_Island" title="Manitoulin Island">Manitoulin Island</a>) to "Grand Lac" (<a href="/wiki/Lake_Superior" title="Lake Superior">Lake Superior</a>) via <a href="/wiki/St._Marys_River_(Michigan%E2%80%93Ontario)" title="St. Marys River (Michigan–Ontario)">St. Mary's River</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Butterfield_56-2"><a href="#cite_note-Butterfield-56">[56]</a></sup></li>
<li>1622 – The <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Dutch</a> ship <i>Leeuwin</i> discovers land near present-day <a href="/wiki/Cape_Leeuwin" title="Cape Leeuwin">Cape Leeuwin</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wood_62-1"><a href="#cite_note-Wood-62">[62]</a></sup></li>
<li>1623 – <a href="/wiki/Jan_Carstenszoon" title="Jan Carstenszoon">Jan Carstenszoon</a> discovers the western coast of Cape York Peninsula from Cape Keerweer to the southern mouth of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gilbert-Einasleigh_River" title="Gilbert-Einasleigh River">Gilbert River</a>; while his consort <b>Willem Joosten van Colster</b> discovers "Arnhemsland" and "Speultsland" (modern <a href="/wiki/Arnhem_Land" title="Arnhem Land">Arnhem Land</a> and perhaps <a href="/wiki/Groote_Eylandt" title="Groote Eylandt">Groote Eylandt</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wood_62-2"><a href="#cite_note-Wood-62">[62]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Peters_64-0"><a href="#cite_note-Peters-64">[64]</a></sup></li>
<li>1624 – <a href="/wiki/Ant%C3%B3nio_de_Andrade" title="António de Andrade">António de Andrade</a> crosses the <a href="/wiki/Himalayas" title="Himalayas">Himalayas</a> through the <a href="/wiki/Mana_Pass" title="Mana Pass">Mana Pass</a> and reaches <a href="/wiki/Tibet" title="Tibet">Tibet</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wessels_51-1"><a href="#cite_note-Wessels-51">[51]</a></sup></li>
<li>1627 – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jesuit" title="Jesuit">Jesuit</a> missionaries <a href="/wiki/Est%C3%AAv%C3%A3o_Cacella" title="Estêvão Cacella">Estêvão Cacella</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jo%C3%A3o_Cabral" title="João Cabral">João Cabral</a> cross the <a href="/wiki/Himalayas" title="Himalayas">Himalayas</a> and are the first to enter <a href="/wiki/Bhutan" title="Bhutan">Bhutan</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wessels_51-2"><a href="#cite_note-Wessels-51">[51]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kapadia_65-0"><a href="#cite_note-Kapadia-65">[65]</a></sup></li>
<li>1627 – <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Thijssen" title="François Thijssen">François Thijssen</a>, accompanied by <a href="/wiki/Pieter_Nuyts" title="Pieter Nuyts">Pieter Nuyts</a>, discovers over 1,609 kilometres (1,000 mi) of coastline east of <a href="/wiki/Cape_Leeuwin" title="Cape Leeuwin">Cape Leeuwin</a> to the eastern end of the <a href="/wiki/Great_Australian_Bight" title="Great Australian Bight">Great Australian Bight</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mutch_53-5"><a href="#cite_note-Mutch-53">[53]</a></sup></li>
<li>1628 – Cabral is the first to enter <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepal</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wessels_51-3"><a href="#cite_note-Wessels-51">[51]</a></sup></li>
<li>1628 – Gerrit Frederikszoon de Witt captain of the <a href="/wiki/Vianen_(ship)" title="Vianen (ship)"><i>Vianen</i></a> discovers "Witsland" about 21° S, sailing 320 kilometres (200 mi) along the coast and discovering <a href="/wiki/Barrow_Island_(Western_Australia)" title="Barrow Island (Western Australia)">Barrow Island</a> and parts of the <a href="/wiki/Dampier_Archipelago" title="Dampier Archipelago">Dampier Archipelago</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wood_62-3"><a href="#cite_note-Wood-62">[62]</a></sup></li>
<li>1628–30 – Vasilii Bugor ascends the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Upper_Tunguska" title="Upper Tunguska">Upper Tunguska</a> and portages to the upper Lena, descending it to its confluence with the <a href="/wiki/Kirenga_River" title="Kirenga River">Kirenga</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lantzeff_46-3"><a href="#cite_note-Lantzeff-46">[46]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fisher1943_52-4"><a href="#cite_note-Fisher1943-52">[52]</a></sup></li>
<li>1631–32 – <a href="/wiki/Luke_Foxe" title="Luke Foxe">Luke Foxe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thomas_James_(sea_captain)" title="Thomas James (sea captain)">Thomas James</a>, in separate expeditions, both circumnavigate Hudson Bay in search of a Northwest Passage; Foxe sails through <a href="/wiki/Foxe_Channel" title="Foxe Channel">the channel</a> and into <a href="/wiki/Foxe_Basin" title="Foxe Basin">the basin</a> now named after him to 66°47′ N, while James winters in the bay <a href="/wiki/James_Bay" title="James Bay">named after him</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Christy_59-1"><a href="#cite_note-Christy-59">[59]</a></sup></li>
<li>1632–33 – <a href="/wiki/Pyotr_Beketov" title="Pyotr Beketov">Pyotr Beketov</a> descends the Lena as far as its great bend, erects the ostrog <a href="/wiki/Yakutsk" title="Yakutsk">Yakutsk</a>, and sends a detachment some 720 kilometres (450 mi) downriver (where the <i>zimovie</i> <a href="/wiki/Zhigansky_District" title="Zhigansky District">Zhigansk</a> is built) and another east up the <a href="/wiki/Aldan_River" title="Aldan River">Aldan</a> as far as the <a href="/wiki/Amga_River" title="Amga River">Amga</a> (which they also ascend in search of <a href="/wiki/Yasak" title="Yasak">yasak</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lantzeff_46-4"><a href="#cite_note-Lantzeff-46">[46]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Forsyth_50-1"><a href="#cite_note-Forsyth-50">[50]</a></sup></li>
<li>1633–34 – <a href="/wiki/Jean_Nicolet" title="Jean Nicolet">Jean Nicolet</a> discovers <a href="/wiki/Lake_Michigan" title="Lake Michigan">Lake Michigan</a> and likely reaches <a href="/wiki/Green_Bay,_Wisconsin" title="Green Bay, Wisconsin">Green Bay, Wisconsin</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fischer_66-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fischer-66">[66]</a></sup></li>
